2632 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
2633 function crosssectionPlotCallback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2634 % Plot 3
2635 
2636 % Get the Application data:
2637 % -------------------------
2638 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
2639 z = guiparams.z;
2640 A = guiparams.A;
2641 % V = guiparams.V;
2642 % Map = guiparams.Map;
2643 
2644 % Preprocess the data:
2645 % --------------------
2646 A = VMT_PreProcess(z,A);
2647 
2648 % Push messages to Log Window:
2649 % ----------------------------
2650 log_text = {'Plotting Cross Section (reprocessing)'};
2651 statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, log_text)
2652 
2653 % Process the transects:
2654 % ----------------------
2655 A(1).hgns = guiparams.horizontal_grid_node_spacing;
2656 A(1).vgns = guiparams.vertical_grid_node_spacing;
2657 A(1).wse  = guiparams.water_surface_elevation;  %Set the WSE to entered value
2658 [A,V,processing_log_text] = VMT_ProcessTransects(z,A,...
2659     guiparams.set_cross_section_endpoints,guiparams.unit_discharge_correction,guiparams.bed_elevation,guiparams.start_bank);
2660 
2661 % Push messages to Log Window:
2662 % ----------------------------
2663 statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, processing_log_text)
2664 
2665 % Plot the cross section:
2666 % -----------------------
2667 log_text = {...
2668     'Cross Section Plotting Parameters';...
2669     sprintf('   Contour variable: %s'          ,guiparams.contours(guiparams.idx_contour).string);...
2670     sprintf('   Vertical exaggeration: %d'     ,guiparams.vertical_exaggeration);...
2671     sprintf('   Vector scale: %3.1f'           ,guiparams.vector_scale_cross_section);...
2672     sprintf('   Horizontal vector spacing: %d' ,guiparams.horizontal_vector_spacing);...
2673     sprintf('   Horz. vector spacing, in ground distance: %g m', (guiparams.horizontal_vector_spacing*guiparams.horizontal_grid_node_spacing));...
2674     sprintf('   Vertical vector spacing: %d'   ,guiparams.vertical_vector_spacing);...
2675     sprintf('   Vert. vector spacing, in ground distance: %g m', (guiparams.vertical_vector_spacing*guiparams.vertical_grid_node_spacing));...
2676     sprintf('   Horizontal smoothing window: %d',guiparams.horizontal_smoothing_window);...
2677     sprintf('   Horz. smoothing window, in ground distance: %g m', (2*guiparams.horizontal_smoothing_window*guiparams.horizontal_grid_node_spacing));...
2678     sprintf('   Vertical smoothing window: %d' ,guiparams.vertical_smoothing_window);...
2679     sprintf('   Vert. smoothing window, in ground distance: %g m', (2*guiparams.vertical_smoothing_window*guiparams.vertical_grid_node_spacing));...
2680     
2681     };
2682 if guiparams.plot_secondary_flow_vectors
2683     log_text = vertcat(log_text, {...
2684         sprintf('   Vector variable: %s',guiparams.secondary_flows(guiparams.idx_secondary_flow_vector_variable).string);...
2685         sprintf('   Inc. vertical component?: %d',guiparams.include_vertical_velocity)...
2686         });
2687 end
2688 % Push messages to Log Window:
2689 % ----------------------------
2690 statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, log_text)
2691 
2692 if guiparams.plot_secondary_flow_vectors
2693     %msgbox('Plotting Cross Section','VMT Status','help','replace')
2694 %     V = VMT_SmoothVar(V, ...
2695 %         ...guiparams.contour, ...
2696 %         guiparams.horizontal_smoothing_window, ...
2697 %         guiparams.vertical_smoothing_window);
2698     V = VMT_SmoothVar(V, ...
2699         ...guiparams.secondary_flow_vector_variable, ...
2700         guiparams.horizontal_smoothing_window, ...
2701         guiparams.vertical_smoothing_window);
2702     [V] = VMT_Vorticity(V);
2703     [~,A,V,guiparams.mcsQuivers,plot_cont_log_text] = VMT_PlotXSContQuiver(z,A,V, ...
2704         guiparams.contour, ...
2705         guiparams.vector_scale_cross_section, ...
2706         guiparams.vertical_exaggeration, ...
2707         guiparams.horizontal_vector_spacing, ...
2708         guiparams.vertical_vector_spacing, ...
2709         guiparams.secondary_flow_vector_variable, ...
2710         guiparams.include_vertical_velocity, ...
2711         guiparams.english_units,...
2712         guiparams.allow_vmt_flip_flux,...
2713         guiparams.start_bank); %#ok<ASGLU> % PLOT3
2714     
2715 elseif ~guiparams.plot_secondary_flow_vectors
2716     V = VMT_SmoothVar(V, ...
2717         ...guiparams.contour, ...
2718         guiparams.horizontal_smoothing_window, ...
2719         guiparams.vertical_smoothing_window);
2720     [V] = VMT_Vorticity(V);
2721     [~,A,V,zmin,zmax,plot_cont_log_text] = VMT_PlotXSCont(z,A,V, ...
2722         guiparams.contour, ...
2723         guiparams.vertical_exaggeration, ...
2724         guiparams.english_units, ...
2725         guiparams.allow_vmt_flip_flux,...
2726         guiparams.start_bank); %#ok<ASGLU> % PLOT3
2727     
2728     guiparams.zmin = zmin;
2729     guiparams.zmax = zmax;
2730     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
2731 end
2732 
2733 % Force plot to be formated properly
2734 % ----------------------------------
2735 if guiparams.presentation
2736     menuStylePresentation_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2737 else
2738     menuStylePrint_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2739 end
2740 switch guiparams.renderer
2741     case 'OpenGL'
2742         menuOpenGL_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2743     case 'painters'
2744         menuPainters_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2745     case 'zbuffer'
2746         menuZbuffer_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2747 end
2748 
2749 % Focus the figure
2750 % ----------------
2751 hff = findobj('name','Mean Cross Section Contour');
2752 if ~isempty(hff) &&  ishandle(hff)
2753     figure(hff)
2754 end
2755 
2756 % Re-store the Application data:
2757 % ------------------------------
2758 guiparams.V = V;
2759 setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
2760 
2761 % Start the Graphics Control Gui
2762 % ------------------------------
2763 VMT_GraphicsControl
2764 
2765 % Push messages to Log Window:
2766 % ----------------------------
2767 statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, plot_cont_log_text)
2768 % msgbox('Plotting Complete','VMT Status','help','replace')
2769 
2770 % [EOF] crosssectionPlotCallback

2777 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
2778 function SaveMATFile_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2779 % saveDataCallback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2780 
2781 % Get the Application data:
2782 % -------------------------
2783 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
2784 z   = guiparams.z;   %#ok<NASGU>
2785 A   = guiparams.A;   %#ok<NASGU>
2786 V   = guiparams.V;   %#ok<NASGU>
2787 Map = guiparams.Map; %#ok<NASGU>
2788 
2789 [the_file,the_path] = ...
2790     uiputfile({'*.mat','MAT-Files (*.mat)'}, ...
2791     'Save MAT-File', ...
2792     fullfile(guiparams.mat_path,guiparams.savefile));
2793 
2794 % Save the processed data to a MAT file:
2795 % --------------------------------------
2796 if ischar(the_file)
2797     guiparams.mat_path = the_path;
2798     guiparams.mat_file = the_file;
2799     guiparams.savefile = the_file;
2800     
2801     % Re-store the Application data:
2802     % ------------------------------
2803     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
2804     
2805     % Update the preferences:
2806     % -----------------------
2807     guiprefs = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
2808     guiprefs.mat_path = the_path;
2809     guiprefs.mat_file = the_file;
2810     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs',guiprefs)
2811     store_prefs(handles.figure1,'mat')
2812     
2813     [~,filename,extension] = fileparts(guiparams.savefile);
2814     savefile = [filename extension];
2815     h = msgbox(['Saving processed data in MAT File ''' savefile ''''], ...
2816         'Saving Processed Data File...'); %#ok<NASGU>
2817     disp('Saving Processed Data File...')
2818     disp(savefile)
2819     save(savefile,'A','V','z','Map')
2820 end

2825 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
2826 function SaveTecplotFile_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2827 
2828 % Get the Application data:
2829 % -------------------------
2830 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
2831 % z   = guiparams.z;
2832 % A   = guiparams.A;
2833 V   = guiparams.V;
2834 % Map = guiparams.Map;
2835 
2836 [the_file,the_path] = ...
2837     uiputfile({'*.dat','Tecplot Files (*.dat)'}, ...
2838     'Save Tecplot File', ...
2839     fullfile(guiparams.tecplot_path,guiparams.tecplot_file));
2840 
2841 % Output the data (no smoothing) to Tecplot:
2842 % ------------------------------------------
2843 if ischar(the_file)
2844     guiparams.tecplot_path = the_path;
2845     guiparams.tecplot_file = the_file;
2846     
2847     % Re-store the Application data:
2848     % ------------------------------
2849     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
2850     
2851     % Update the preferences:
2852     % -----------------------
2853     guiprefs = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
2854     guiprefs.tecplot_path = the_path;
2855     guiprefs.tecplot_file = the_file;
2856     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs',guiprefs)
2857     store_prefs(handles.figure1,'tecplot')
2858     
2859     % Push to log window
2860     % ------------------
2861     log_text = {...
2862         'Exporting Data to Tecplot (*.dat) File...';...
2863         'Directory:';...
2864         the_path;...
2865         ['Filename: ' the_file]};
2866     statusLogging(handles.LogWindow,log_text)
2867         
2868     if isempty(V)
2869         A = guiparams.A;
2870         A(1).hgns = guiparams.horizontal_grid_node_spacing;
2871         A(1).vgns = guiparams.vertical_grid_node_spacing;
2872         A(1).wse  = guiparams.water_surface_elevation;  %Set the WSE to entered value
2873         [A,V,processing_log_text] = VMT_ProcessTransects(z,A,...
2874     guiparams.set_cross_section_endpoints,guiparams.unit_discharge_correction,guiparams.bed_elevation,guiparams.start_bank);
2875     end
2876     VMT_BuildTecplotFile(V,fullfile(guiparams.tecplot_path,guiparams.tecplot_file));
2877     
2878     % Push to log window
2879     % ------------------
2880     log_text = {'Exporting XS Bathy Data to Tecplot (*.dat) File...'};
2881     statusLogging(handles.LogWindow,log_text)
2882     
2883     VMT_BuildTecplotFile_XSBathy(V,fullfile(guiparams.tecplot_path,guiparams.tecplot_file));
2884     
2885     % Push to log window
2886     % ------------------
2887     log_text = {'Tecplot Export Complete'};
2888     statusLogging(handles.LogWindow,log_text)
2889    
2890 end

2955 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
2956 function ExportMultibeamBathymetry_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2957 
2958 % Get the Application data:
2959 % -------------------------
2960 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
2961 guiprefs  = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
2962 z = guiparams.z;
2963 A = guiparams.A;
2964 V = guiparams.V; %#ok<NASGU>
2965 % Map = guiparams.Map;
2966 setends = guiparams.set_cross_section_endpoints;
2967 
2968 [the_file,the_path] = ...
2969     uiputfile({'*.csv','Multibeam Bathymetry Files (*.csv)'}, ...
2970     'Export Multibeam Bathymetry', ...
2971     fullfile(guiprefs.multibeambathymetry_path, ...
2972     guiprefs.multibeambathymetry_file));
2973 
2974 if ischar(the_file)
2975     guiparams.multibeambathymetry_path = the_path;
2976     guiparams.multibeambathymetry_file = the_file;
2977     
2978     % Re-store the Application data:
2979     % ------------------------------
2980     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
2981     
2982     % Update the preferences:
2983     % -----------------------
2984     guiprefs = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
2985     guiprefs.multibeambathymetry_path = the_path;
2986     guiprefs.multibeambathymetry_file = the_file;
2987     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs',guiprefs)
2988     store_prefs(handles.figure1,'multibeambathymetry')
2989     
2990     if guiparams.output_auxiliary_data
2991     end
2992     
2993     %msgbox('Processing Bathymetry...Please Be Patient','VMT Status','help','replace')
2994     
2995     savefile = fullfile(guiparams.multibeambathymetry_path, ...
2996         guiparams.multibeambathymetry_file);
2997     
2998     log_text = {'Multibeam bathymetry file saved to:';...
2999         ['   ' savefile]};
3000     statusLogging(handles.LogWindow,log_text)
3001     
3002     % Process the transects:
3003     % ----------------------
3004     A(1).hgns = guiparams.horizontal_grid_node_spacing;
3005     A(1).vgns = guiparams.vertical_grid_node_spacing;
3006     A(1).wse  = guiparams.water_surface_elevation;  %Set the WSE to entered value
3007     [A,V,processing_log_text] = VMT_ProcessTransects(z,A,...
3008     guiparams.set_cross_section_endpoints,guiparams.unit_discharge_correction,guiparams.bed_elevation,guiparams.start_bank);
3009     
3010     % Compute the smoothed variables
3011     % ------------------------------
3012     % This is required so that the V struc is complete at any point during
3013     % runtime.
3014     V = VMT_SmoothVar(V, ...
3015         ...guiparams.contour, ...
3016         guiparams.horizontal_smoothing_window, ...
3017         guiparams.vertical_smoothing_window);
3018     [V] = VMT_Vorticity(V);
3019     % Push messages to Log Window:
3020     % ----------------------------
3021     statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, processing_log_text)
3022 
3023     
3024     VMT_MBBathy(guiparams.z, ...
3025         guiparams.A, ...
3026         savefile, ...
3027         guiparams.beam_angle, ...
3028         guiparams.magnetic_variation, ...
3029         guiparams.water_surface_elevation, ...
3030         guiparams.output_auxiliary_data);
3031     
3032     %msgbox('Bathymetry Output Complete','VMT Status','help','replace')
3033     
3034 end
3035 
3036 % [EOF] ExportMultibeamBathymetry_Callback

3039 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
3040 function BeamAngle_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
3041 % Get the beam angle
3042 
3043 % Get the Application data:
3044 % -------------------------
3045 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
3046 
3047 % Get the new entry and make sure it is valid (numeric, positive):
3048 % ----------------------------------------------------------------
3049 new_beam_angle = str2double(get(hObject,'String'));
3050 is_a_number = ~isnan(new_beam_angle);
3051 is_positive = new_beam_angle>=0;
3052 
3053 % Modify the Application data:
3054 % ----------------------------
3055 if is_a_number && is_positive
3056     guiparams.beam_angle = new_beam_angle;
3057     
3058     % Re-store the Application data:
3059     % ------------------------------
3060     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
3061     
3062 else % Reject the (incorrect) input
3063     set(hObject,'String',guiparams.beam_angle)
3064 end

3637 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
3638 function SaveLog_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
3639 
3640 % Get the Application data:
3641 % -------------------------
3642 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
3643 guiprefs  = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
3644 % z   = guiparams.z;   %#ok<NASGU>
3645 % A   = guiparams.A;   %#ok<NASGU>
3646 % V   = guiparams.V;   %#ok<NASGU>
3647 % Map = guiparams.Map; %#ok<NASGU>
3648 
3649 [the_file,the_path] = ...
3650     uiputfile({'*.txt','TXT-Files (*.txt)'}, ...
3651     'Choose where to save the log file', ...
3652     fullfile(guiprefs.log_path,guiprefs.log_file));
3653 
3654 % Save the log to a TXT file:
3655 % ---------------------------
3656 if ischar(the_file)
3657     guiparams.log_path = the_path;
3658     guiparams.log_file = the_file;
3659     %guiparams.savefile = the_file;
3660     
3661     % Re-store the Application data:
3662     % ------------------------------
3663     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
3664     
3665     % Update the preferences:
3666     % -----------------------
3667     guiprefs = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
3668     guiprefs.log_path = the_path;
3669     guiprefs.log_file = the_file;
3670     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs',guiprefs)
3671     store_prefs(handles.figure1,'log')
3672     
3673     [~,filename,extension] = fileparts(the_file);
3674     savefile = [the_path filename extension];
3675     h = msgbox(['Saving log to: ''' savefile ''''], ...
3676         'Saving Log File...'); %#ok<NASGU>
3677     
3678     logfile = get(handles.LogWindow,'string');
3679     [nrows,~]= size(logfile);
3680     fid = fopen(savefile, 'w');
3681     for row=1:nrows
3682         fprintf(fid, '%s \n', logfile{row,:});
3683     end
3684     fclose(fid);
3685 end
3686 % [EOF] SaveLog_Callback
3687

3693 function handles = buildToolbar(handles)
3694 
3695 icons = getIcons;

3697 
3698 % Load data
3699 % icon = imread('C:\Users\pfricker\Desktop\icons\file_open.png');
3700 % icon = double(icon)/(2^16-1);
3701 % icon(icon==0) = NaN;

3800 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
3801 function load_prefs(hfigure)
3802 % Load the GUI preferences.  Also, initialize preferences if they don't
3803 % already exist.
3804 
3805 % Preferences:
3806 % 'ascii'                Path and filenames of current ASCII files
3807 % 'mat'                  Path and filename of current MAT file
3808 % 'tecplot'              Path and filename of last Tecplot file
3809 % 'kmz'                  Path and filename of last KMZ file
3810 % 'multibeambathymetry'  Path and filename of last Multibeam Bathymetry file
3811 % 'log'                  Path and filename of last Log file
3812 % 'iric'                 Path and filename of last iRic ANV file
3813 % 'excel'                Path and filename of last Excel file
3814 % 'aerial'               Path and filename of last Aerial file
3815 % 'shoreline'            Path and filename of last Shoreline file
3816 % 'renderer'             Default graphics renderer
3817 % 'units'                Default plotting units
3818 % 'plotref'              Default plotting vertical reference
3819 % 'runcounter'           Keeps a running tally of how many times VMT is
3820 %                        started
3821 % 'setendpoints'         Path and filename of user set endpoints
3822 
3823 % Originals
3824 % prefs = {'ascii2gispath' 'ascii2kmlpath' 'asciipath'   'doqqpath' ...
3825 %          'endspath'      'logpath'       'matpath'     'savedpath' ...
3826 %          'shorepath'     'stapath'       'ysidatapath' 'ysidatapath'};
3827 
3828 % ASCII

3833     else
3834         guiprefs.ascii_path = pwd;
3835     end
3836     does_exist = false(1,length(ascii.file));
3837     for k = 1:length(ascii.file) % Check each file one-by-one
3838         does_exist(k) = exist(fullfile(ascii.path,ascii.file{k}),'file');
3839     end
3840     if any(does_exist)
3841         guiprefs.ascii_file = ascii.file(does_exist);
3842     else
3843         guiprefs.ascii_file = {''};
3844     end
3845 else % Initialize ASCII
3846     guiprefs.ascii_path = pwd;
3847     guiprefs.ascii_file = {''};

4159 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
4160 function store_prefs(hfigure,pref)
4161 % Store preferences in the Application data and in the persistent
4162 % preferences data.
4163 
4164 % Preferences:
4165 % 'ascii'                Path and filenames of current ASCII files
4166 % 'mat'                  Path and filename of current MAT file
4167 % 'tecplot'              Path and filename of last Tecplot file
4168 % 'kmz'                  Path and filename of last KMZ file
4169 % 'multibeambathymetry'  Path and filename of last Multibeam Bathymetry file
4170 % 'log'                  Path and filename of last Log file
4171 % 'iric'                 Path and filename of last iRic ANV file
4172 % 'excel'                Path and filename of last Excel file
4173 % 'aerial'               Path and filename of last Aerial file
4174 % 'shoreline'            Path and filename of last Shoreline file
4175 % 'renderer'             Default graphics renderer
4176 % 'units'                Default plotting units
4177 % 'plotref'              Default plotting vertical reference
4178 % 'runcounter'           Keeps a running tally of how many times VMT is
4179 %                        started
4180 % 'setendpoints'         Path and filename of user endpoint file
4181 
4182 guiprefs = getappdata(hfigure,'guiprefs');
4183 
4184 switch pref
4185     case 'ascii'
4186         ascii.path = guiprefs.ascii_path;
4187         ascii.file = guiprefs.ascii_file;
4188         setpref('VMT','ascii',ascii)
4189     case 'mat'
4190         mat.path = guiprefs.mat_path;
4191         mat.file = guiprefs.mat_file;
4192         setpref('VMT','mat',mat)
4193     case 'tecplot'
4194         tecplot.path = guiprefs.tecplot_path;
4195         tecplot.file = guiprefs.tecplot_file;
4196         setpref('VMT','tecplot',tecplot)
4197     case 'kmz'
4198         kmz.path = guiprefs.kmz_path;
4199         kmz.file = guiprefs.kmz_file;
4200         setpref('VMT','kmz',kmz)
4201     case 'multibeambathymetry'
4202         multibeambathymetry.path = guiprefs.multibeambathymetry_path;
4203         multibeambathymetry.file = guiprefs.multibeambathymetry_file;
4204         setpref('VMT','multibeambathymetry',multibeambathymetry)
4205     case 'log'
4206         log.path = guiprefs.log_path;
4207         log.file = guiprefs.log_file;
4208         setpref('VMT','log',log)
4209     case 'iric'
4210         iric.path = guiprefs.iric_path;
4211         iric.file = guiprefs.iric_file;
4212         setpref('VMT','iric',iric)
4213     case 'excel'
4214         excel.path = guiprefs.excel_path;
4215         excel.file = guiprefs.excel_file;
4216         setpref('VMT','excel',excel)
4217     case 'aerial'
4218         aerial.path = guiprefs.aerial_path;
4219         aerial.file = guiprefs.aerial_file;
4220         setpref('VMT','aerial',aerial)
4221     case 'shoreline'
4222         shoreline.path = guiprefs.shoreline_path;
4223         shoreline.file = guiprefs.shoreline_file;
4224         setpref('VMT','shoreline',shoreline)
4225     case 'renderer'
4226         renderer = guiprefs.renderer;
4227         setpref('VMT','renderer',renderer)
4228     case 'units'
4229         units = guiprefs.units;
4230         setpref('VMT','units',units)
4231     case 'plotref'
4232         plotref = guiprefs.plotref;
4233         setpref('VMT','plotref',plotref)
4234     case 'runcounter'
4235         runcounter = guiprefs.runcounter;
4236         setpref('VMT','runcounter',runcounter)
4237     case 'setendpoints'
4238         setendpoints.path = guiprefs.setendpoints_path;
4239         setendpoints.file = guiprefs.setendpoints_file;
4240         setpref('VMT','setendpoints',setendpoints)
4241     otherwise
4242 end
4243 
4244 % if ismember(pref,prefs)
4245 %     setpref('VMT',pref,value)
4246 %
4247 %     guiprefs = getappdata(hfigure,'guiprefs');
4248 %     guiprefs.(pref) = value;
4249 %     setappdata(hfigure,'guiprefs',guiprefs)
4250 % end
4251 
4252 % [EOF] store_prefs

4255 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
4256 function initGUI(handles)
4257 % Initialize the UI controls in the GUI.
4258 
4259 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
4260 
4261 % Set the name and version
4262 set(handles.figure1,'Name',['Velocity Mapping Toolbox (VMT) ' guiparams.vmt_version{1}], ...
4263     'DockControls','off')
4264 %set(handles.VMTversion,             'String',guiparams.vmt_version)
4265 
4266 % Set the PLOT 1 axis labels
4267 axes(handles.Plot1Shiptracks);
4268 set(handles.Plot1Shiptracks,'DataAspectRatio',[1 1 1],'PlotBoxAspectRatio',[1 1 1])
4269 xlabel('UTM Easting (m)')
4270 ylabel('UTM Northing (m)')
4271 box on
4272 grid on
4273 % ticks_format('%6.0f','%8.0f'); %formats the ticks for UTM
4274 
4275 %%%%%%%%%%%%
4276 % MENU BAR %
4277 %%%%%%%%%%%%
4278 if guiparams.english_units
4279     set(handles.menuMetric, 'Checked','off')
4280     set(handles.menuEnglish,'Checked','on')
4281 else
4282     set(handles.menuMetric, 'Checked','on')
4283     set(handles.menuEnglish,'Checked','off')
4284 end
4285 
4286 if guiparams.set_cross_section_endpoints
4287     set(handles.menuCrossSectionEndpointAutomatic,'Checked','off')
4288     set(handles.menuCrossSectionEndpointManual,   'Checked','on')
4289 else
4290     set(handles.menuCrossSectionEndpointAutomatic,'Checked','on')
4291     set(handles.menuCrossSectionEndpointManual,   'Checked','off')
4292 end
4293 
4294 
4295 if guiparams.print
4296     set(handles.menuPrintFormat,       'Checked','on')
4297     set(handles.menuPresentationFormat,'Checked','off')
4298     set(handles.menuStylePrint,        'Checked','on')
4299     set(handles.menuStylePresentation, 'Checked','off')
4300 elseif guiparams.presentation
4301     set(handles.menuPrintFormat,       'Checked','off')
4302     set(handles.menuPresentationFormat,'Checked','on')
4303     set(handles.menuStylePrint,        'Checked','off')
4304     set(handles.menuStylePresentation, 'Checked','on')
4305 else
4306 end
4307 
4308 switch guiparams.renderer
4309     case 'OpenGL'
4310         set(handles.menuOpenGL,        'Checked','on')
4311         set(handles.menuPainters,      'Checked','off')
4312         set(handles.menuZbuffer,       'Checked','off')
4313     case 'painters'
4314         set(handles.menuOpenGL,        'Checked','off')
4315         set(handles.menuPainters,      'Checked','on')
4316         set(handles.menuZbuffer,       'Checked','off')
4317     case 'zbuffer'
4318         set(handles.menuOpenGL,        'Checked','off')
4319         set(handles.menuPainters,      'Checked','off')
4320         set(handles.menuZbuffer,       'Checked','on')
4321 end
4322 
4323 
4324 %%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
4325 % DATA EXPORT %
4326 %%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
4327 % BathymetryPanel
4328 % set(handles.BeamAngle,                  'String',guiparams.beam_angle)
4329 % set(handles.MagneticVariation,          'String',guiparams.magnetic_variation)
4330 % set(handles.WSE,                        'String',guiparams.wse)
4331 % set(handles.OutputAuxiliaryData,        'Value', guiparams.output_auxiliary_data)
4332 
4333 %%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
4334 % PLOTTING/PLAN VIEW %
4335 %%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
4336 % PlanViewPanel
4337 set(handles.DepthRangeMin,              'String',guiparams.depth_range_min)
4338 set(handles.DepthRangeMax,              'String',guiparams.depth_range_max)
4339 set(handles.VectorScalePlanView,        'String',guiparams.vector_scale_plan_view)
4340 set(handles.VectorSpacingPlanview,      'String',guiparams.vector_spacing_plan_view)
4341 set(handles.SmoothingWindowSize,        'String',guiparams.smoothing_window_size)
4342 set(handles.AddBackground,              'Value', guiparams.add_background)
4343 
4344 
4345 %%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
4346 % PLOTTING/SHIP TRACKS %
4347 %%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
4348 % ShiptracksPanel
4349 set(handles.HorizontalGridNodeSpacing,  'String',guiparams.horizontal_grid_node_spacing)
4350 set(handles.VerticalGridNodeSpacing,    'String',guiparams.vertical_grid_node_spacing)
4351 %set(handles.SetCrossSectionEndpoints,   'Value', guiparams.set_cross_section_endpoints)
4352 
4353 %%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
4354 % PLOTTING/CROSS SECTIONS %
4355 %%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
4356 % CrossSectionsPanel
4357 set(handles.Contour,                    'String',{guiparams.contours.string}, ...
4358     'Value', guiparams.idx_contour)
4359 set(handles.VerticalExaggeration,       'String',guiparams.vertical_exaggeration)
4360 set(handles.VectorScaleCrossSection,    'String',guiparams.vector_scale_cross_section)
4361 set(handles.HorizontalVectorSpacing,    'String',guiparams.horizontal_vector_spacing)
4362 set(handles.VerticalVectorSpacing,      'String',guiparams.vertical_vector_spacing)
4363 set(handles.HorizontalSmoothingWindow,  'String',guiparams.horizontal_smoothing_window)
4364 set(handles.VerticalSmoothingWindow,    'String',guiparams.vertical_smoothing_window)
4365 set(handles.PlotSecondaryFlowVectors,   'Value', guiparams.plot_secondary_flow_vectors)
4366 set(handles.SecondaryFlowVectorVariable,'String',{guiparams.secondary_flows.string}, ...
4367     'Value', guiparams.idx_secondary_flow_vector_variable)
4368 set(handles.IncludeVerticalVelocity,    'Value', guiparams.include_vertical_velocity)
4369 
4370 % set(handles.EnglishUnits,               'Value',guiparams.english_units)
4371 
4372 % [EOF] initGUI

4375 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
4376 function set_enable(handles,enable_state)
4377 
4378 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
4379 
4380 switch enable_state
4381     case 'init'
4382         guiparams.gui_state = 'init';
4383         set([handles.menuFile
4384             handles.menuOpen
4385             handles.menuOpenASCII
4386             handles.menuOpenMAT
4387             ],'Enable','on')
4388         
4389         set([handles.toolbarLoadData
4390             ],'Enable','on')
4391         set([handles.toolbarSaveMatFile
4392             handles.toolbarSaveBathymetry
4393             handles.toolbarSaveFigures
4394             handles.toolbarSaveExcel
4395             handles.toolbarPlottingParameters
4396             handles.toolbarProcessingParameters
4397             ],'Enable','off')
4398         
4399         set([handles.DepthRangeMin
4400             handles.DepthRangeMax
4401             handles.VectorScalePlanView
4402             handles.VectorSpacingPlanview
4403             handles.SmoothingWindowSize
4404             handles.AddBackground
4405             handles.PlotPlanView
4406             ],'Enable','off')
4407       
4408         set([handles.HorizontalGridNodeSpacing
4409             handles.VerticalGridNodeSpacing
4410             handles.PlotShiptracks
4411             ],'Enable','off')
4412         
4413         set([handles.Contour
4414             handles.VerticalExaggeration
4415             handles.VectorScaleCrossSection
4416             handles.HorizontalVectorSpacing
4417             handles.VerticalVectorSpacing
4418             handles.HorizontalSmoothingWindow
4419             handles.VerticalSmoothingWindow
4420             handles.PlotSecondaryFlowVectors
4421             handles.SecondaryFlowVectorVariable
4422             handles.IncludeVerticalVelocity
4423             handles.IncludeVerticalVelocityText
4424             handles.PlotCrossSection
4425             ],'Enable','off')
4426         
4427     case 'fileloaded'
4428         guiparams.gui_state = 'fileloaded';
4429         set([handles.menuFile
4430             handles.menuOpen
4431             handles.menuOpenASCII
4432             handles.menuOpenMAT
4433             handles.menuSaveMAT
4434             handles.menuSaveTecplot
4435             handles.menuSaveKMZFile
4436             handles.menuSettings
4437             handles.menuPlottingParameters
4438             handles.menuMetric

4712 function dialogUnits(hObject,eventdata,handles,the_units)
4713 
4714 dialog_params = getappdata(handles.Figure,'dialog_params');

4716     case 'metric'

4718         
4719         set(handles.UnitsMetric, 'Value',1)
4720         set(handles.UnitsEnglish,'Value',0)

4722         dialog_params.english_units = true;
4723         
4724         set(handles.UnitsMetric, 'Value',0)
4725         set(handles.UnitsEnglish,'Value',1)
4726     otherwise
4727 end

4770 end

5025 % Position the dialog and make it visible:
5026 % ----------------------------------------
5027 fpos = get(hf,'Position');
5028 dpos = [(fpos(1) + fpos(3)/2 -w/2) (fpos(2) + fpos(4)/2)];
5029 movegui(handles.Figure,dpos)
5030 set(handles.Figure,'Visible','on')
5031 
5032 % Hold the dialog open:
5033 % ---------------------
5034 waitfor(handles.OK)
5035 
5036 % Return the outputs and close the dialog:
5037 % ----------------------------------------
5038 dialog_params = getappdata(handles.Figure,'dialog_params');
5039 selected_figures = dialog_params.selected_figures;
5040 
5041 delete(handles.Figure)
5042 
5043 % [EOF] openFiguresDialog
5044 
5045 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
5046 function dialogSelectFigures(hObject,eventdata,handles)
5047 
5048 dialog_params = getappdata(handles.Figure,'dialog_params');
5049 
5050 idx_selected = get(handles.Figures,'Value');
5051 fig_names    = get(handles.Figures,'String');
5052 selected     = fig_names(idx_selected);
5053 dialog_params.selected_figures = selected;
5054 
5055 setappdata(handles.Figure,'dialog_params',dialog_params)
5056

5482 function guiparams = createGUIparams
5483 % Creates the guiparams structure with specified defaults.

5488 guiprefs = getpref('VMT');

5723 % --- Hidden keyboard commands
5724 function figure1_WindowKeyPressFcn(hObject, eventdata, handles)
5725 % Used to pass specific hidden keyboard commands to VMT. Currently, the
5726 % only use for this function is to open Beta support for SonTek M9 data.
5727 %
5728 % hObject    handle to figure1 (see GCBO)
5729 % eventdata  structure with the following fields (see FIGURE)
5730 %    Key: name of the key that was pressed, in lower case
5731 %    Character: character interpretation of the key(s) that was pressed
5732 %    Modifier: name(s) of the modifier key(s) (i.e., control, shift) pressed
5733 % handles    structure with handles and user data (see GUIDATA)
5734 
5735 in1 = eventdata.Modifier; 
5736 in2 = eventdata.Key;
5737 
5738 if ~isempty(in1) % User pressed at least one modifier key
5739     input = [in1{:} in2];
5740 else
5741     input = in2;
5742 end
5743 
5744 switch input
5745     % Hidden SonTek M9 support
5746     case 'shiftcontrols'
5747         msgtxt = {...
5748             'VMT offers limited support for SonTek M9/S5 data.';...
5749             'SonTek RiverSurveyorLive required data format:';...
5750             '      -ENU coordinates';...
5751             '      -Desired GPS reference (BT/GGA/VTG)'
5752             '';...
5753             'Abosolutely NO GUARANTEE is made or implied that this';...
5754             'functionality will work for all cases. Results are';...
5755             'PROVISIONAL at best.'};
5756         msgbox(msgtxt, 'Hidden Functionality: Process SonTek M9', 'warn','replace')
5757         
5758         % Get the Application data:
5759         % -------------------------
5760         guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
5761         guiprefs = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
5762         
5763         % Ask the user to select files:
5764         % -----------------------------
5765         % current_file = fullfile(guiparams.data_folder,guiparams.data_files{1});
5766         % current_file = fullfile(guiprefs.mat_path,guiprefs.mat_file);
5767         if iscell(guiprefs.mat_file)
5768             uifile = fullfile(guiprefs.mat_path,guiprefs.mat_file{1});
5769         else
5770             uifile = fullfile(guiprefs.mat_path,guiprefs.mat_file);
5771         end
5772         [filename,pathname] = ...
5773             uigetfile({'*.mat','MAT-files (*.mat)'}, ...
5774             'Select SonTek RiverSurveyor Live v3.60 MAT File', ...
5775             uifile, 'MultiSelect','on');
5776         
5777         if ischar(pathname) % The user did not hit "Cancel"
5778             guiparams.data_folder = pathname;
5779             if ischar(filename)
5780                 filename = {filename};
5781             end
5782             guiparams.data_files = filename;
5783             guiparams.mat_file = '';
5784             
5785             setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
5786             
5787             
5788             
5789             % Update the preferences:
5790             % -----------------------
5791             guiprefs = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
5792             guiprefs.ascii_path = pathname;
5793             guiprefs.ascii_file = filename;
5794             setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs',guiprefs)
5795             store_prefs(handles.figure1,'ascii')
5796             
5797             % Push messages to Log Window:
5798             % ----------------------------
5799             log_text = {...
5800                 '';...
5801                 ['%--- ' datestr(now) ' ---%'];...
5802                 'Current Project Directory:';...
5803                 guiparams.data_folder;
5804                 'Loading the following files into memory:';...
5805                 char(filename)};
5806             statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, log_text)
5807             
5808             % Read the file(s)
5809             % ----------------
5810             %A = parseSonTekVMT(fullfile(pathname,filename));
5811             
5812             [~,~,savefile,A,z] = ...
5813                 VMT_ReadFiles_SonTek(guiparams.data_folder,guiparams.data_files);
5814             guiparams.savefile = savefile;
5815             guiparams.A        = A;
5816             guiparams.z        = z;
5817             setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
5818             
5819             
5820             % Update the GUI:
5821             % ---------------
5822             set_enable(handles,'fileloaded')
5823         end  
5824     case 'shiftcontroll' % Call SontekMAT2KML
5825         SontekMAT2KML;
5826     case 'f1' % Call the VMT UsersGuide
5827         menuUsersGuide_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
5828         
5829     case 'controlalte'
5830         VMT_BuildCustomFlatFile;
5831     otherwise
5832         %disp(input)
5833 end
